         from flask import Flask, render_template, redirect, url_for, request
         import os
         
         app = Flask(__name__)
         app.config['SECRET_KEY'] = 'dev-secret-key'
         
         DATA_DIR = 'data'
         
         # Utility functions
         
         def read_devices(username=None):
             devices = []
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'devices.txt')
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) < 13:
                             continue
                         device = {
                             'username': parts[0],
                             'device_id': int(parts[1]),
                             'device_name': parts[2],
                             'device_type': parts[3],
                             'room': parts[4],
                             'brand': parts[5],
                             'model': parts[6],
                             'status': parts[7],
                             'power': parts[8],
                             'brightness': parts[9],
                             'temperature': parts[10],
                             'mode': parts[11],
                             'schedule_time': parts[12],
                         }
                         if username is None or device['username'] == username:
                             devices.append(device)
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return devices
         
         def save_devices(devices):
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'devices.txt')
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for d in devices:
                         line = '|'.join([
                             d['username'],
                             str(d['device_id']),
                             d['device_name'],
                             d['device_type'],
                             d['room'],
                             d['brand'],
                             d['model'],
                             d['status'],
                             d['power'],
                             d['brightness'],
                             d['temperature'],
                             d['mode'],
                             d['schedule_time'],
                         ]) + '\n'
                         f.write(line)
             except Exception:
                 pass
         
         def read_rooms(username=None):
             rooms = []
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'rooms.txt')
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) < 3:
                             continue
                         room = {
                             'username': parts[0],
                             'room_id': int(parts[1]),
                             'room_name': parts[2],
                         }
                         if username is None or room['username'] == username:
                             rooms.append(room)
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return rooms
         
         def read_automation_rules(username=None):
             rules = []
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'automation_rules.txt')
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) < 9:
                             continue
                         rule = {
                             'username': parts[0],
                             'rule_id': int(parts[1]),
                             'rule_name': parts[2],
                             'trigger_type': parts[3],
                             'trigger_value': parts[4],
                             'action_device_id': int(parts[5]),
                             'action_type': parts[6],
                             'action_value': parts[7],
                             'enabled': parts[8].lower() == 'true',
                         }
                         if username is None or rule['username'] == username:
                             rules.append(rule)
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return rules
         
         def save_automation_rules(rules):
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'automation_rules.txt')
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for r in rules:
                         line = '|'.join([
                             r['username'],
                             str(r['rule_id']),
                             r['rule_name'],
                             r['trigger_type'],
                             r['trigger_value'],
                             str(r['action_device_id']),
                             r['action_type'],
                             r['action_value'],
                             'true' if r['enabled'] else 'false',
                         ]) + '\n'
                         f.write(line)
             except Exception:
                 pass
         
         def read_energy_logs(username=None):
             records = []
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'energy_logs.txt')
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) < 4:
                             continue
                         record = {
                             'username': parts[0],
                             'device_id': int(parts[1]),
                             'date': parts[2],
                             'consumption_kwh': float(parts[3]),
                         }
                         if username is None or record['username'] == username:
                             records.append(record)
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return records
         
         def read_activity_logs(username=None):
             logs = []
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'activity_logs.txt')
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) < 5:
                             continue
                         log = {
                             'username': parts[0],
                             'timestamp': parts[1],
                             'device_id': int(parts[2]),
                             'action': parts[3],
                             'details': parts[4],
                         }
                         if username is None or log['username'] == username:
                             logs.append(log)
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return logs
         
         # Helpers
         
         def get_next_device_id(devices):
             if not devices:
                 return 1
             return max(d['device_id'] for d in devices) + 1
         
         def get_next_rule_id(rules):
             if not rules:
                 return 1
             return max(r['rule_id'] for r in rules) + 1
         
         DEFAULT_USERNAME = 'john_doe'
         
         # 1. Root Route
         @app.route('/', methods=['GET'])
         def root_redirect():
             return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))
         
         # 2. Dashboard
         @app.route('/dashboard', methods=['GET'])
         def dashboard():
             username = DEFAULT_USERNAME
             devices = read_devices(username)
             rooms = read_rooms(username)
         
             total_devices = len(devices)
             active_devices = sum(1 for d in devices if d['status'].lower() == 'online')
             offline_devices = total_devices - active_devices
         
             rooms_count = {r['room_name']: 0 for r in rooms}
             for d in devices:
                 if d['room'] in rooms_count:
                     rooms_count[d['room']] += 1
         
             return render_template('dashboard.html', total_devices=total_devices, active_devices=active_devices, offline_devices=offline_devices, rooms=rooms_count)
         
         # 3. Device List
         @app.route('/devices', methods=['GET'])
         def device_list():
             username = DEFAULT_USERNAME
             devices_all = read_devices(username)
             devices = [{
                 'device_id': d['device_id'],
                 'device_name': d['device_name'],
                 'device_type': d['device_type'],
                 'room': d['room'],
                 'status': d['status'],
             } for d in devices_all]
             return render_template('device_list.html', devices=devices)
         
         # 4. Add Device
         @app.route('/device/add', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def add_device():
             username = DEFAULT_USERNAME
             devices = read_devices(username)
             rooms = read_rooms(username)
         
             device_types = sorted(set(d['device_type'] for d in devices))
             room_names = sorted(set(r['room_name'] for r in rooms))
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 device_name = request.form.get('device_name', '').strip()
                 device_type = request.form.get('device_type', '').strip()
                 room = request.form.get('device_room', '').strip()
         
                 if not device_name or not device_type or not room:
                     # Missing fields, re-render GET
                     return render_template('add_device.html', device_types=device_types, rooms=room_names)
         
                 new_device_id = get_next_device_id(devices)
                 new_device = {
                     'username': username,
                     'device_id': new_device_id,
                     'device_name': device_name,
                     'device_type': device_type,
                     'room': room,
                     'brand': '',
                     'model': '',
                     'status': 'Offline',
                     'power': 'off',
                     'brightness': '',
                     'temperature': '',
                     'mode': '',
                     'schedule_time': '',
                 }
                 devices.append(new_device)
                 save_devices(devices)
                 return redirect(url_for('device_list'))
         
             return render_template('add_device.html', device_types=device_types, rooms=room_names)
         
         # 5. Device Control
         @app.route('/device/<int:device_id>/control', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def device_control(device_id):
             username = DEFAULT_USERNAME
             devices = read_devices(username)
             device = next((d for d in devices if d['device_id'] == device_id and d['username'] == username), None)
             if device is None:
                 return redirect(url_for('device_list'))
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 power = request.form.get('power')
                 brightness = request.form.get('brightness', '')
                 temperature = request.form.get('temperature', '')
                 mode = request.form.get('mode', '')
                 schedule_time = request.form.get('schedule_time', '')
         
                 if power in ('on', 'off'):
                     device['power'] = power
                     device['status'] = 'Online' if power == 'on' else 'Offline'
         
                 device['brightness'] = brightness
                 device['temperature'] = temperature
                 device['mode'] = mode
                 device['schedule_time'] = schedule_time
         
                 save_devices(devices)
                 return redirect(url_for('device_control', device_id=device_id))
         
             device_ctx = {
                 'device_id': device['device_id'],
                 'device_name': device['device_name'],
                 'status': device['status'],
                 'power': device['power'],
                 'brightness': device['brightness'],
                 'temperature': device['temperature'],
                 'mode': device['mode'],
                 'schedule_time': device['schedule_time'],
             }
             return render_template('device_control.html', device=device_ctx)
         
         # 6. Automation Rules
         @app.route('/automation', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def automation():
             username = DEFAULT_USERNAME
             rules = read_automation_rules(username)
             devices = read_devices(username)
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 rule_name = request.form.get('rule_name', '').strip()
                 trigger_type = request.form.get('trigger_type', '').strip()
                 trigger_value = request.form.get('trigger_value', '').strip()
                 action_device_id_str = request.form.get('action_device', '').strip()
                 action_type = request.form.get('action_type', '').strip()
         
                 if rule_name and trigger_type and action_device_id_str.isdigit() and action_type:
                     action_device_id = int(action_device_id_str)
                     new_rule_id = get_next_rule_id(rules)
                     new_rule = {
                         'username': username,
                         'rule_id': new_rule_id,
                         'rule_name': rule_name,
                         'trigger_type': trigger_type,
                         'trigger_value': trigger_value,
                         'action_device_id': action_device_id,
                         'action_type': action_type,
                         'action_value': '',
                         'enabled': True,
                     }
                     rules.append(new_rule)
                     save_automation_rules(rules)
                     return redirect(url_for('automation'))
         
             devices_select = [{'device_id': d['device_id'], 'device_name': d['device_name']} for d in devices]
             return render_template('automation.html', automation_rules=rules, devices=devices_select)
         
         # 7. Energy Report
         @app.route('/energy', methods=['GET'])
         def energy():
             username = DEFAULT_USERNAME
             energy_records = read_energy_logs(username)
             devices = read_devices(username)
         
             device_name_map = {d['device_id']: d['device_name'] for d in devices}
         
             date_filter = request.args.get('date_filter')
         
             filtered_records = []
             for record in energy_records:
                 if date_filter and record['date'] != date_filter:
                     continue
                 filtered_records.append({
                     'username': record['username'],
                     'device_id': record['device_id'],
                     'device_name': device_name_map.get(record['device_id'], ''),
                     'date': record['date'],
                     'consumption_kwh': record['consumption_kwh'],
                 })
         
             return render_template('energy.html', energy_records=filtered_records, date_filter=date_filter)
         
         # 8. Activity Logs
         @app.route('/activity', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def activity_logs():
             username = DEFAULT_USERNAME
             logs = read_activity_logs(username)
         
             search_query = None
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 search_query = request.form.get('search_query', '').strip()
                 if search_query:
                     logs = [log for log in logs if search_query.lower() in log['action'].lower() or search_query.lower() in log['details'].lower() or search_query.lower() in log['username'].lower()]
         
             return render_template('activity_logs.html', logs=logs, search_query=search_query)
         
         if __name__ == '__main__':
             app.run(debug=True, port=5000)

         from flask import Flask, render_template, redirect, url_for, request
         import os
         
         app = Flask(__name__)
         app.config['SECRET_KEY'] = 'dev-secret-key'
         
         DATA_DIR = 'data'
         
         # Utility functions for data file handling
         
         def read_devices(username=None):
             devices = []
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'devices.txt')
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) < 13:
                             continue  # skip malformed lines
                         d = {
                             'username': parts[0],
                             'device_id': int(parts[1]),
                             'device_name': parts[2],
                             'device_type': parts[3],
                             'room': parts[4],
                             'brand': parts[5],
                             'model': parts[6],
                             'status': parts[7],
                             'power': parts[8],
                             'brightness': parts[9],
                             'temperature': parts[10],
                             'mode': parts[11],
                             'schedule_time': parts[12],
                         }
                         if username is None or d['username'] == username:
                             devices.append(d)
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return devices
         
         
         def save_devices(devices):
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'devices.txt')
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for d in devices:
                         line = '|'.join([
                             d['username'],
                             str(d['device_id']),
                             d['device_name'],
                             d['device_type'],
                             d['room'],
                             d['brand'],
                             d['model'],
                             d['status'],
                             d['power'],
                             d['brightness'],
                             d['temperature'],
                             d['mode'],
                             d['schedule_time']]) + '\n'
                         f.write(line)
             except Exception:
                 pass
         
         
         def read_rooms(username=None):
             rooms = []
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'rooms.txt')
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) < 3:
                             continue
                         r = {
                             'username': parts[0],
                             'room_id': int(parts[1]),
                             'room_name': parts[2],
                         }
                         if username is None or r['username'] == username:
                             rooms.append(r)
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return rooms
         
         
         def read_automation_rules(username=None):
             rules = []
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'automation_rules.txt')
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) < 9:
                             continue
                         rule = {
                             'username': parts[0],
                             'rule_id': int(parts[1]),
                             'rule_name': parts[2],
                             'trigger_type': parts[3],
                             'trigger_value': parts[4],
                             'action_device_id': int(parts[5]),
                             'action_type': parts[6],
                             'action_value': parts[7],
                             'enabled': parts[8].lower() == 'true'
                         }
                         if username is None or rule['username'] == username:
                             rules.append(rule)
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return rules
         
         
         def save_automation_rules(rules):
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'automation_rules.txt')
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for r in rules:
                         line = '|'.join([
                             r['username'],
                             str(r['rule_id']),
                             r['rule_name'],
                             r['trigger_type'],
                             r['trigger_value'],
                             str(r['action_device_id']),
                             r['action_type'],
                             r['action_value'],
                             'true' if r['enabled'] else 'false'
                         ]) + '\n'
                         f.write(line)
             except Exception:
                 pass
         
         
         def read_energy_logs(username=None):
             records = []
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'energy_logs.txt')
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) < 4:
                             continue
                         record = {
                             'username': parts[0],
                             'device_id': int(parts[1]),
                             'date': parts[2],
                             'consumption_kwh': float(parts[3]),
                         }
                         if username is None or record['username'] == username:
                             records.append(record)
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return records
         
         
         def read_activity_logs(username=None):
             logs = []
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'activity_logs.txt')
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) < 5:
                             continue
                         log = {
                             'username': parts[0],
                             'timestamp': parts[1],
                             'device_id': int(parts[2]),
                             'action': parts[3],
                             'details': parts[4],
                         }
                         if username is None or log['username'] == username:
                             logs.append(log)
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return logs
         
         
         # Helper for unique ids
         
         def get_next_device_id(devices):
             if not devices:
                 return 1
             return max(d['device_id'] for d in devices) + 1
         
         def get_next_rule_id(rules):
             if not rules:
                 return 1
             return max(r['rule_id'] for r in rules) + 1
         
         
         # Application default user
         DEFAULT_USERNAME = 'john_doe'
         
         
         # 1. Root Route
         @app.route('/', methods=['GET'])
         def root_redirect():
             return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))
         
         
         # 2. Dashboard Page
         @app.route('/dashboard', methods=['GET'])
         def dashboard():
             username = DEFAULT_USERNAME
             devices = read_devices(username)
             rooms = read_rooms(username)
         
             total_devices = len(devices)
             active_devices = sum(1 for d in devices if d['status'].lower() == 'online')
             offline_devices = total_devices - active_devices
         
             # Room name to device count
             rooms_count = {}
             for r in rooms:
                 rooms_count[r['room_name']] = 0
             for d in devices:
                 if d['room'] in rooms_count:
                     rooms_count[d['room']] += 1
         
             return render_template('dashboard.html',
                                    total_devices=total_devices,
                                    active_devices=active_devices,
                                    offline_devices=offline_devices,
                                    rooms=rooms_count)
         
         
         # 3. Device List Page
         @app.route('/devices', methods=['GET'])
         def device_list():
             username = DEFAULT_USERNAME
             devices_all = read_devices(username)
             # Provide only keys required by page
             devices = []
             for d in devices_all:
                 devices.append({
                     'device_id': d['device_id'],
                     'device_name': d['device_name'],
                     'device_type': d['device_type'],
                     'room': d['room'],
                     'status': d['status'],
                 })
             return render_template('device_list.html', devices=devices)
         
         
         # 4. Add Device Page
         @app.route('/device/add', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def add_device():
             username = DEFAULT_USERNAME
             device_types = set()
             rooms_list = []
         
             devices_all = read_devices(username)
             rooms = read_rooms(username)
         
             # Get unique device types from existing devices
             for d in devices_all:
                 device_types.add(d['device_type'])
             device_types = sorted(device_types)
         
             # Get list of room names
             rooms_list = sorted({r['room_name'] for r in rooms})
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 device_name = request.form.get('device_name', '').strip()
                 device_type = request.form.get('device_type', '').strip()
                 room = request.form.get('device_room', '').strip()
         
                 # Validate required fields
                 if not device_name or not device_type or not room:
                     # Re-render with error? Spec does not mention error handling. Just return.
                     return render_template('add_device.html', device_types=device_types, rooms=rooms_list)
         
                 # Assign new device_id
                 new_id = get_next_device_id(devices_all)
         
                 # Default values for new device
                 brand = ''
                 model = ''
                 status = 'Offline'
                 power = 'off'
                 brightness = ''
                 temperature = ''
                 mode = ''
                 schedule_time = ''
         
                 new_device = {
                     'username': username,
                     'device_id': new_id,
                     'device_name': device_name,
                     'device_type': device_type,
                     'room': room,
                     'brand': brand,
                     'model': model,
                     'status': status,
                     'power': power,
                     'brightness': brightness,
                     'temperature': temperature,
                     'mode': mode,
                     'schedule_time': schedule_time,
                 }
         
                 devices_all.append(new_device)
                 save_devices(devices_all)
         
                 return redirect(url_for('device_list'))
         
             # GET method
             return render_template('add_device.html', device_types=device_types, rooms=rooms_list)
         
         
         # 5. Device Control Page
         @app.route('/device/<int:device_id>/control', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def device_control(device_id):
             username = DEFAULT_USERNAME
             devices_all = read_devices(username)
             device = None
             for d in devices_all:
                 if d['device_id'] == device_id and d['username'] == username:
                     device = d
                     break
             if device is None:
                 # Device not found, redirect to device list
                 return redirect(url_for('device_list'))
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 # Update fields from form
                 # Spec does not prescribe exact form fields except power toggle and settings
                 # We will handle power, brightness, temperature, mode, schedule_time if present
         
                 power = request.form.get('power')
                 brightness = request.form.get('brightness', '')
                 temperature = request.form.get('temperature', '')
                 mode = request.form.get('mode', '')
                 schedule_time = request.form.get('schedule_time', '')
         
                 if power in ('on', 'off'):
                     device['power'] = power
                     device['status'] = 'Online' if power == 'on' else 'Offline'
         
                 # Update optional fields if provided
                 device['brightness'] = brightness
                 device['temperature'] = temperature
                 device['mode'] = mode
                 device['schedule_time'] = schedule_time
         
                 # Save back
                 save_devices(devices_all)
         
                 # After POST, redirect to same control page (reload)
                 return redirect(url_for('device_control', device_id=device_id))
         
             # GET method
             # Provide required keys plus all available for template
             device_ctx = {
                 'device_id': device['device_id'],
                 'device_name': device['device_name'],
                 'status': device['status'],
                 'power': device['power'],
                 'brightness': device['brightness'],
                 'temperature': device['temperature'],
                 'mode': device['mode'],
                 'schedule_time': device['schedule_time'],
             }
         
             return render_template('device_control.html', device=device_ctx)
         
         
         # 6. Automation Rules Page
         @app.route('/automation', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def automation():
             username = DEFAULT_USERNAME
             rules = read_automation_rules(username)
             devices_all = read_devices(username)
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 # Add or update rules - the spec does not clarify update details so we'll assume add only
         
                 rule_name = request.form.get('rule_name', '').strip()
                 trigger_type = request.form.get('trigger_type', '').strip()
                 trigger_value = request.form.get('trigger_value', '').strip()
                 action_device_id_str = request.form.get('action_device', '').strip()
                 action_type = request.form.get('action_type', '').strip()
         
                 if not rule_name or not trigger_type or not action_device_id_str or not action_type:
                     # Missing required fields, re-render
                     pass  # Just continue to render with existing
                 else:
                     try:
                         action_device_id = int(action_device_id_str)
                     except ValueError:
                         action_device_id = None
         
                     if action_device_id is not None:
                         # New rule_id
                         new_id = get_next_rule_id(rules)
                         new_rule = {
                             'username': username,
                             'rule_id': new_id,
                             'rule_name': rule_name,
                             'trigger_type': trigger_type,
                             'trigger_value': trigger_value,
                             'action_device_id': action_device_id,
                             'action_type': action_type,
                             'action_value': '',
                             'enabled': True
                         }
                         rules.append(new_rule)
                         save_automation_rules(rules)
                         return redirect(url_for('automation'))
         
             # GET or default render
             # provide devices with device_id and device_name
             devices = [{'device_id': d['device_id'], 'device_name': d['device_name']} for d in devices_all]
         
             return render_template('automation.html', automation_rules=rules, devices=devices)
         
         
         # 7. Energy Report Page
         @app.route('/energy', methods=['GET'])
         def energy():
             username = DEFAULT_USERNAME
             energy_records = read_energy_logs(username)
             devices = read_devices(username)
         
             # Enrich energy_records with device_name
             device_name_map = {d['device_id']: d['device_name'] for d in devices}
         
             # Optional date filter
             date_filter = request.args.get('date_filter', None)
         
             filtered_records = []
             for r in energy_records:
                 if date_filter and r['date'] != date_filter:
                     continue
                 dev_name = device_name_map.get(r['device_id'], '')
                 rec = {
                     'username': r['username'],
                     'device_id': r['device_id'],
                     'device_name': dev_name,
                     'date': r['date'],
                     'consumption_kwh': r['consumption_kwh'],
                 }
                 filtered_records.append(rec)
         
             return render_template('energy.html', energy_records=filtered_records, date_filter=date_filter)
         
         
         # 8. Activity Logs Page
         @app.route('/activity', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def activity_logs():
             username = DEFAULT_USERNAME
             logs = read_activity_logs(username)
         
             search_query = None
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 search_query = request.form.get('search_query', '').strip()
                 if search_query:
                     logs = [log for log in logs if search_query.lower() in log['action'].lower() or search_query.lower() in log['details'].lower() or search_query.lower() in log['username'].lower()]
         
             return render_template('activity_logs.html', logs=logs, search_query=search_query)
         
         
         if __name__ == '__main__':
             app.run(debug=True, port=5000)

         from flask import Flask, render_template, redirect, url_for, request
         import os
         
         app = Flask(__name__)
         app.config['SECRET_KEY'] = 'dev-secret-key'
         
         DATA_DIR = 'data'
         
         # Data file handling utilities
         
         def read_devices(username=None):
             devices = []
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'devices.txt')
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) < 13:
                             continue
                         device = {
                             'username': parts[0],
                             'device_id': int(parts[1]),
                             'device_name': parts[2],
                             'device_type': parts[3],
                             'room': parts[4],
                             'brand': parts[5],
                             'model': parts[6],
                             'status': parts[7],
                             'power': parts[8],
                             'brightness': parts[9],
                             'temperature': parts[10],
                             'mode': parts[11],
                             'schedule_time': parts[12],
                         }
                         if username is None or device['username'] == username:
                             devices.append(device)
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return devices
         
         
         def save_devices(devices):
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'devices.txt')
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for d in devices:
                         line = '|'.join([
                             d['username'],
                             str(d['device_id']),
                             d['device_name'],
                             d['device_type'],
                             d['room'],
                             d['brand'],
                             d['model'],
                             d['status'],
                             d['power'],
                             d['brightness'],
                             d['temperature'],
                             d['mode'],
                             d['schedule_time'],
                         ]) + '\n'
                         f.write(line)
             except Exception:
                 pass
         
         
         def read_rooms(username=None):
             rooms = []
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'rooms.txt')
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) < 3:
                             continue
                         room = {
                             'username': parts[0],
                             'room_id': int(parts[1]),
                             'room_name': parts[2],
                         }
                         if username is None or room['username'] == username:
                             rooms.append(room)
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return rooms
         
         
         def read_automation_rules(username=None):
             rules = []
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'automation_rules.txt')
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) < 9:
                             continue
                         rule = {
                             'username': parts[0],
                             'rule_id': int(parts[1]),
                             'rule_name': parts[2],
                             'trigger_type': parts[3],
                             'trigger_value': parts[4],
                             'action_device_id': int(parts[5]),
                             'action_type': parts[6],
                             'action_value': parts[7],
                             'enabled': parts[8].lower() == 'true',
                         }
                         if username is None or rule['username'] == username:
                             rules.append(rule)
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return rules
         
         
         def save_automation_rules(rules):
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'automation_rules.txt')
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for r in rules:
                         line = '|'.join([
                             r['username'],
                             str(r['rule_id']),
                             r['rule_name'],
                             r['trigger_type'],
                             r['trigger_value'],
                             str(r['action_device_id']),
                             r['action_type'],
                             r['action_value'],
                             'true' if r['enabled'] else 'false',
                         ]) + '\n'
                         f.write(line)
             except Exception:
                 pass
         
         
         def read_energy_logs(username=None):
             energy_records = []
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'energy_logs.txt')
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) < 4:
                             continue
                         record = {
                             'username': parts[0],
                             'device_id': int(parts[1]),
                             'date': parts[2],
                             'consumption_kwh': float(parts[3]),
                         }
                         if username is None or record['username'] == username:
                             energy_records.append(record)
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return energy_records
         
         
         def read_activity_logs(username=None):
             logs = []
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'activity_logs.txt')
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) < 5:
                             continue
                         log = {
                             'username': parts[0],
                             'timestamp': parts[1],
                             'device_id': int(parts[2]),
                             'action': parts[3],
                             'details': parts[4],
                         }
                         if username is None or log['username'] == username:
                             logs.append(log)
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return logs
         
         
         # Helper functions
         
         def get_next_device_id(devices):
             if not devices:
                 return 1
             return max(d['device_id'] for d in devices) + 1
         
         
         def get_next_rule_id(rules):
             if not rules:
                 return 1
             return max(r['rule_id'] for r in rules) + 1
         
         
         DEFAULT_USERNAME = 'john_doe'
         
         
         # 1. Root Route
         @app.route('/', methods=['GET'])
         def root_redirect():
             return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))
         
         
         # 2. Dashboard Page
         @app.route('/dashboard', methods=['GET'])
         def dashboard():
             username = DEFAULT_USERNAME
             devices = read_devices(username)
             rooms = read_rooms(username)
         
             total_devices = len(devices)
             active_devices = sum(1 for d in devices if d['status'].lower() == 'online')
             offline_devices = total_devices - active_devices
         
             room_device_counts = {r['room_name']: 0 for r in rooms}
             for d in devices:
                 if d['room'] in room_device_counts:
                     room_device_counts[d['room']] += 1
         
             return render_template(
                 'dashboard.html',
                 total_devices=total_devices,
                 active_devices=active_devices,
                 offline_devices=offline_devices,
                 rooms=room_device_counts
             )
         
         
         # 3. Device List Page
         @app.route('/devices', methods=['GET'])
         def device_list():
             username = DEFAULT_USERNAME
             all_devices = read_devices(username)
             devices = [
                 {
                     'device_id': d['device_id'],
                     'device_name': d['device_name'],
                     'device_type': d['device_type'],
                     'room': d['room'],
                     'status': d['status'],
                 } for d in all_devices
             ]
             return render_template('device_list.html', devices=devices)
         
         
         # 4. Add Device Page
         @app.route('/device/add', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def add_device():
             username = DEFAULT_USERNAME
             devices = read_devices(username)
             rooms = read_rooms(username)
         
             device_types = sorted(set(d['device_type'] for d in devices))
             room_names = sorted(set(r['room_name'] for r in rooms))
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 device_name = request.form.get('device_name', '').strip()
                 device_type = request.form.get('device_type', '').strip()
                 room = request.form.get('device_room', '').strip()
         
                 if not device_name or not device_type or not room:
                     # Missing required fields, just re-render GET with lists
                     return render_template('add_device.html', device_types=device_types, rooms=room_names)
         
                 new_device_id = get_next_device_id(devices)
         
                 new_device = {
                     'username': username,
                     'device_id': new_device_id,
                     'device_name': device_name,
                     'device_type': device_type,
                     'room': room,
                     'brand': '',
                     'model': '',
                     'status': 'Offline',
                     'power': 'off',
                     'brightness': '',
                     'temperature': '',
                     'mode': '',
                     'schedule_time': '',
                 }
         
                 devices.append(new_device)
                 save_devices(devices)
         
                 return redirect(url_for('device_list'))
         
             # GET method
             return render_template('add_device.html', device_types=device_types, rooms=room_names)
         
         
         # 5. Device Control Page
         @app.route('/device/<int:device_id>/control', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def device_control(device_id):
             username = DEFAULT_USERNAME
             devices = read_devices(username)
             device = next((d for d in devices if d['device_id'] == device_id and d['username'] == username), None)
             if device is None:
                 return redirect(url_for('device_list'))
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 power = request.form.get('power')
                 brightness = request.form.get('brightness', '')
                 temperature = request.form.get('temperature', '')
                 mode = request.form.get('mode', '')
                 schedule_time = request.form.get('schedule_time', '')
         
                 if power in ('on', 'off'):
                     device['power'] = power
                     device['status'] = 'Online' if power == 'on' else 'Offline'
         
                 device['brightness'] = brightness
                 device['temperature'] = temperature
                 device['mode'] = mode
                 device['schedule_time'] = schedule_time
         
                 save_devices(devices)
         
                 return redirect(url_for('device_control', device_id=device_id))
         
             device_context = {
                 'device_id': device['device_id'],
                 'device_name': device['device_name'],
                 'status': device['status'],
                 'power': device['power'],
                 'brightness': device['brightness'],
                 'temperature': device['temperature'],
                 'mode': device['mode'],
                 'schedule_time': device['schedule_time'],
             }
             return render_template('device_control.html', device=device_context)
         
         
         # 6. Automation Rules Page
         @app.route('/automation', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def automation():
             username = DEFAULT_USERNAME
             rules = read_automation_rules(username)
             devices = read_devices(username)
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 rule_name = request.form.get('rule_name', '').strip()
                 trigger_type = request.form.get('trigger_type', '').strip()
                 trigger_value = request.form.get('trigger_value', '').strip()
                 action_device_id_str = request.form.get('action_device', '').strip()
                 action_type = request.form.get('action_type', '').strip()
         
                 if rule_name and trigger_type and action_device_id_str.isdigit() and action_type:
                     action_device_id = int(action_device_id_str)
                     new_rule_id = get_next_rule_id(rules)
                     new_rule = {
                         'username': username,
                         'rule_id': new_rule_id,
                         'rule_name': rule_name,
                         'trigger_type': trigger_type,
                         'trigger_value': trigger_value,
                         'action_device_id': action_device_id,
                         'action_type': action_type,
                         'action_value': '',  # Empty as per spec
                         'enabled': True
                     }
                     rules.append(new_rule)
                     save_automation_rules(rules)
                     return redirect(url_for('automation'))
         
             device_select_list = [{'device_id': d['device_id'], 'device_name': d['device_name']} for d in devices]
             return render_template('automation.html', automation_rules=rules, devices=device_select_list)
         
         
         # 7. Energy Report Page
         @app.route('/energy', methods=['GET'])
         def energy():
             username = DEFAULT_USERNAME
             energy_records = read_energy_logs(username)
             devices = read_devices(username)
         
             device_name_map = {d['device_id']: d['device_name'] for d in devices}
         
             date_filter = request.args.get('date_filter')
         
             filtered_records = []
             for record in energy_records:
                 if date_filter and record['date'] != date_filter:
                     continue
                 filtered_records.append({
                     'username': record['username'],
                     'device_id': record['device_id'],
                     'device_name': device_name_map.get(record['device_id'], ''),
                     'date': record['date'],
                     'consumption_kwh': record['consumption_kwh'],
                 })
         
             return render_template('energy.html', energy_records=filtered_records, date_filter=date_filter)
         
         
         # 8. Activity Logs Page
         @app.route('/activity', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def activity_logs():
             username = DEFAULT_USERNAME
             logs = read_activity_logs(username)
         
             search_query = None
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 search_query = request.form.get('search_query', '').strip()
                 if search_query:
                     logs = [log for log in logs if search_query.lower() in log['action'].lower() or search_query.lower() in log['details'].lower() or search_query.lower() in log['username'].lower()]
         
             return render_template('activity_logs.html', logs=logs, search_query=search_query)
         
         
         if __name__ == '__main__':
             app.run(debug=True, port=5000)

         from flask import Flask, render_template, redirect, url_for, request
         import os
         
         app = Flask(__name__)
         app.config['SECRET_KEY'] = 'dev-secret-key'
         
         DATA_DIR = 'data'
         
         # Utility functions
         
         def read_devices(username=None):
             devices = []
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'devices.txt')
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) < 13:
                             continue
                         device = {
                             'username': parts[0],
                             'device_id': int(parts[1]),
                             'device_name': parts[2],
                             'device_type': parts[3],
                             'room': parts[4],
                             'brand': parts[5],
                             'model': parts[6],
                             'status': parts[7],
                             'power': parts[8],
                             'brightness': parts[9],
                             'temperature': parts[10],
                             'mode': parts[11],
                             'schedule_time': parts[12],
                         }
                         if username is None or device['username'] == username:
                             devices.append(device)
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return devices
         
         def save_devices(devices):
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'devices.txt')
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for d in devices:
                         line = '|'.join([
                             d['username'],
                             str(d['device_id']),
                             d['device_name'],
                             d['device_type'],
                             d['room'],
                             d['brand'],
                             d['model'],
                             d['status'],
                             d['power'],
                             d['brightness'],
                             d['temperature'],
                             d['mode'],
                             d['schedule_time'],
                         ]) + '\n'
                         f.write(line)
             except Exception:
                 pass
         
         def read_rooms(username=None):
             rooms = []
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'rooms.txt')
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) < 3:
                             continue
                         room = {
                             'username': parts[0],
                             'room_id': int(parts[1]),
                             'room_name': parts[2],
                         }
                         if username is None or room['username'] == username:
                             rooms.append(room)
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return rooms
         
         def read_automation_rules(username=None):
             rules = []
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'automation_rules.txt')
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) < 9:
                             continue
                         rule = {
                             'username': parts[0],
                             'rule_id': int(parts[1]),
                             'rule_name': parts[2],
                             'trigger_type': parts[3],
                             'trigger_value': parts[4],
                             'action_device_id': int(parts[5]),
                             'action_type': parts[6],
                             'action_value': parts[7],
                             'enabled': parts[8].lower() == 'true',
                         }
                         if username is None or rule['username'] == username:
                             rules.append(rule)
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return rules
         
         def save_automation_rules(rules):
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'automation_rules.txt')
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for r in rules:
                         line = '|'.join([
                             r['username'],
                             str(r['rule_id']),
                             r['rule_name'],
                             r['trigger_type'],
                             r['trigger_value'],
                             str(r['action_device_id']),
                             r['action_type'],
                             r['action_value'],
                             'true' if r['enabled'] else 'false',
                         ]) + '\n'
                         f.write(line)
             except Exception:
                 pass
         
         def read_energy_logs(username=None):
             records = []
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'energy_logs.txt')
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) < 4:
                             continue
                         record = {
                             'username': parts[0],
                             'device_id': int(parts[1]),
                             'date': parts[2],
                             'consumption_kwh': float(parts[3]),
                         }
                         if username is None or record['username'] == username:
                             records.append(record)
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return records
         
         def read_activity_logs(username=None):
             logs = []
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'activity_logs.txt')
             try:
                 with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) < 5:
                             continue
                         log = {
                             'username': parts[0],
                             'timestamp': parts[1],
                             'device_id': int(parts[2]),
                             'action': parts[3],
                             'details': parts[4],
                         }
                         if username is None or log['username'] == username:
                             logs.append(log)
             except FileNotFoundError:
                 pass
             return logs
         
         # Helpers
         
         def get_next_device_id(devices):
             if not devices:
                 return 1
             return max(d['device_id'] for d in devices) + 1
         
         def get_next_rule_id(rules):
             if not rules:
                 return 1
             return max(r['rule_id'] for r in rules) + 1
         
         DEFAULT_USERNAME = 'john_doe'
         
         # 1. Root Route
         @app.route('/', methods=['GET'])
         def root_redirect():
             return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))
         
         # 2. Dashboard
         @app.route('/dashboard', methods=['GET'])
         def dashboard():
             username = DEFAULT_USERNAME
             devices = read_devices(username)
             rooms = read_rooms(username)
         
             total_devices = len(devices)
             active_devices = sum(1 for d in devices if d['status'].lower() == 'online')
             offline_devices = total_devices - active_devices
         
             rooms_count = {r['room_name']: 0 for r in rooms}
             for d in devices:
                 if d['room'] in rooms_count:
                     rooms_count[d['room']] += 1
         
             return render_template('dashboard.html', total_devices=total_devices, active_devices=active_devices, offline_devices=offline_devices, rooms=rooms_count)
         
         # 3. Device List
         @app.route('/devices', methods=['GET'])
         def device_list():
             username = DEFAULT_USERNAME
             devices_all = read_devices(username)
             devices = [{
                 'device_id': d['device_id'],
                 'device_name': d['device_name'],
                 'device_type': d['device_type'],
                 'room': d['room'],
                 'status': d['status'],
             } for d in devices_all]
             return render_template('device_list.html', devices=devices)
         
         # 4. Add Device
         @app.route('/device/add', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def add_device():
             username = DEFAULT_USERNAME
             devices = read_devices(username)
             rooms = read_rooms(username)
         
             device_types = sorted(set(d['device_type'] for d in devices))
             room_names = sorted(set(r['room_name'] for r in rooms))
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 device_name = request.form.get('device_name', '').strip()
                 device_type = request.form.get('device_type', '').strip()
                 room = request.form.get('device_room', '').strip()
         
                 if not device_name or not device_type or not room:
                     # Missing fields, re-render GET
                     return render_template('add_device.html', device_types=device_types, rooms=room_names)
         
                 new_device_id = get_next_device_id(devices)
                 new_device = {
                     'username': username,
                     'device_id': new_device_id,
                     'device_name': device_name,
                     'device_type': device_type,
                     'room': room,
                     'brand': '',
                     'model': '',
                     'status': 'Offline',
                     'power': 'off',
                     'brightness': '',
                     'temperature': '',
                     'mode': '',
                     'schedule_time': '',
                 }
                 devices.append(new_device)
                 save_devices(devices)
                 return redirect(url_for('device_list'))
         
             return render_template('add_device.html', device_types=device_types, rooms=room_names)
         
         # 5. Device Control
         @app.route('/device/<int:device_id>/control', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def device_control(device_id):
             username = DEFAULT_USERNAME
             devices = read_devices(username)
             device = next((d for d in devices if d['device_id'] == device_id and d['username'] == username), None)
             if device is None:
                 return redirect(url_for('device_list'))
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 power = request.form.get('power')
                 brightness = request.form.get('brightness', '')
                 temperature = request.form.get('temperature', '')
                 mode = request.form.get('mode', '')
                 schedule_time = request.form.get('schedule_time', '')
         
                 if power in ('on', 'off'):
                     device['power'] = power
                     device['status'] = 'Online' if power == 'on' else 'Offline'
         
                 device['brightness'] = brightness
                 device['temperature'] = temperature
                 device['mode'] = mode
                 device['schedule_time'] = schedule_time
         
                 save_devices(devices)
                 return redirect(url_for('device_control', device_id=device_id))
         
             device_ctx = {
                 'device_id': device['device_id'],
                 'device_name': device['device_name'],
                 'status': device['status'],
                 'power': device['power'],
                 'brightness': device['brightness'],
                 'temperature': device['temperature'],
                 'mode': device['mode'],
                 'schedule_time': device['schedule_time'],
             }
             return render_template('device_control.html', device=device_ctx)
         
         # 6. Automation Rules
         @app.route('/automation', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def automation():
             username = DEFAULT_USERNAME
             rules = read_automation_rules(username)
             devices = read_devices(username)
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 rule_name = request.form.get('rule_name', '').strip()
                 trigger_type = request.form.get('trigger_type', '').strip()
                 trigger_value = request.form.get('trigger_value', '').strip()
                 action_device_id_str = request.form.get('action_device', '').strip()
                 action_type = request.form.get('action_type', '').strip()
         
                 if rule_name and trigger_type and action_device_id_str.isdigit() and action_type:
                     action_device_id = int(action_device_id_str)
                     new_rule_id = get_next_rule_id(rules)
                     new_rule = {
                         'username': username,
                         'rule_id': new_rule_id,
                         'rule_name': rule_name,
                         'trigger_type': trigger_type,
                         'trigger_value': trigger_value,
                         'action_device_id': action_device_id,
                         'action_type': action_type,
                         'action_value': '',
                         'enabled': True,
                     }
                     rules.append(new_rule)
                     save_automation_rules(rules)
                     return redirect(url_for('automation'))
         
             devices_select = [{'device_id': d['device_id'], 'device_name': d['device_name']} for d in devices]
             return render_template('automation.html', automation_rules=rules, devices=devices_select)
         
         # 7. Energy Report
         @app.route('/energy', methods=['GET'])
         def energy():
             username = DEFAULT_USERNAME
             energy_records = read_energy_logs(username)
             devices = read_devices(username)
         
             device_name_map = {d['device_id']: d['device_name'] for d in devices}
         
             date_filter = request.args.get('date_filter')
         
             filtered_records = []
             for record in energy_records:
                 if date_filter and record['date'] != date_filter:
                     continue
                 filtered_records.append({
                     'username': record['username'],
                     'device_id': record['device_id'],
                     'device_name': device_name_map.get(record['device_id'], ''),
                     'date': record['date'],
                     'consumption_kwh': record['consumption_kwh'],
                 })
         
             return render_template('energy.html', energy_records=filtered_records, date_filter=date_filter)
         
         # 8. Activity Logs
         @app.route('/activity', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def activity_logs():
             username = DEFAULT_USERNAME
             logs = read_activity_logs(username)
         
             search_query = None
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 search_query = request.form.get('search_query', '').strip()
                 if search_query:
                     logs = [log for log in logs if search_query.lower() in log['action'].lower() or search_query.lower() in log['details'].lower() or search_query.lower() in log['username'].lower()]
         
             return render_template('activity_logs.html', logs=logs, search_query=search_query)
         
         if __name__ == '__main__':
             app.run(debug=True, port=5000)
